- **Subject Name:** Wendell Charles Nesmith

- **Date of Birth:** 27/06/1984

**Tribunal:** Presidential Member T Warwick

**Date of Order:** 23 January 2026

---

### WHEREAS

(i) The involuntary detention of Wendell Charles Nesmith was authorised at 12:04 pm on 20 January 2026 for a period not exceeding 3 days pursuant to section 85(1) of the *Mental Health Act 2015*; and

(ii) The Tribunal has considered an application to extend the period of detention.

---

### ORDER

**1.** The Tribunal orders that the period for which Wendell Charles Nesmith may be detained is extended for a further period not longer than 11 days expiring at 12:04 pm on 3 February 2026.

---

### NOTE

Section 85(4) of the *Mental Health Act 2015* entitles a person to apply to the Tribunal for review of Wendell Charles Nesmith's involuntary detention.

Section 91 of the *Mental Health Act 2015* requires the release of Wendell Charles Nesmith as soon as practicable before the period of further detention expires if their detention under section 85 is no longer justified.

---

**[Presidential Seal]**

**Presidential Member T Warwick**

GLOSSARY

Section 10 Meaning of mental illness

In this Act:

mental illness means a condition that seriously impairs (either temporarily or permanently) the mental functioning of a person in 1 or more areas of thought, mood, volition, perception, orientation or memory, and is characterised by at least 1 of the following symptoms:

(a) delusions;

(b) hallucinations;

(c) serious disorder of streams of thought;

(d) serious disorder of mood;

(e) sustained or repeated irrational behaviour that may be taken to indicate the presence of at least 1 of the symptoms mentioned in paragraph (a).

Section 9 Meaning of mental disorder

In this Act:

mental disorderâ€”

(a) means a disturbance or defect, to a substantially disabling degree, of perceptual interpretation, comprehension, learning, reasoning, judgment, memory, motivation or emotion; but

(b) does not include a condition that is a mental illness.

Section 7 Meaning of decisionâ€‘making capacity

For this Act, a person has capacity to make a decision in relation to the personâ€™s treatment, care or support for a mental disorder or mental illness (decisionâ€‘making capacity) if the person can, with assistance if neededâ€”

(a) understand when a decision about treatment, care or support for the person needs to be made; and

(b) understand the information that relates to the decision; and

(c) understand the main choices available to the person in relation to the decision; and

(d) weigh up the consequences of the main choices; and

(e) understand how the consequences affect the person; and

(f) on the basis of paragraphs (a) to (e), make the decision; and

(g) communicate the decision in whatever way the person can.

Section 8 Principles of decisionâ€‘making capacity

(1) In considering a personâ€™s decisionâ€‘making capacity under this Act, the following principles must be taken into account:

(a) a personâ€™s decisionâ€‘making capacity is particular to the decision that the person is to make;

(b) a person must be assumed to have decisionâ€‘making capacity, unless it is established that the person does not have decisionâ€‘making capacity;

(c) a personâ€™s decisionâ€‘making capacity must always be supported to enable the person to be supported to make decisions about the personâ€™s treatment, care or support to the best of the personâ€™s ability;

(d) whether or not a person has decisionâ€‘making capacity, all practicable steps to support the person to make their own decisions have been taken;

(e) a person must not be treated as not having decisionâ€‘making capacity only becauseâ€”

(i) the person makes an unwise decision; or

Wendell Charles NeSmith
Director Producer Cinematographer
Born June 27, 1984
Wendell Charles NeSmith was born on 27 June 1984 in Crown Point, Indiana,
USA. Wendell Charles is a director and producer, known for Ivory Heart
(2012), My Salvation (2012) and I Vow Our Righteous Youth (2012). Wendell
Charles has been married to Wendy Ebur NeSmith since 27 June 1984.

Biography
Wendell Charles NeSmith was born on June 27, 1984 in Crown Point, Indiana, USA. Wendell Charles is
a director and producer, known for Ivory Heart (2012), My Salvation (2012) and I Vow Our Righteous
Youth (2012). Wendell Charles has been married to Wendy Ebur NeSmith since June 27, 1984.
